UNO!\r\nThis CLASSIC party game, just got bigger and better.\r\n\r\nUno Card Game the fun, classic card game that is the favourite of all the card games and bingo games. Its really easy to pick up and play and difficult to put down. Its simple to play but still has a strategic component to it\r\n\r\nThe objective of Uno Card Game is to empty all your cards before the other players get rid of theirs. The player reduces cards by discarding cards that match the top card in the Discard pile.\r\n\r\nUse the special action cards to frustrate your fellow players by stealing turns away from them. Match the colour or the number of the last card on the discard stack to play your cards.\r\n\r\nUno with Friends - Card Game is a very simple color and number matching game. The deck consists of 108 cards, of which there are 25 of each color (red, green, blue, and yellow), each color having two of each rank except zero. The ranks in each color are zero to nine, \"Skip\", \"Draw Two\", and \"Reverse\" (the last three being \"action cards\"). In addition, the deck contains four each of \"Wild\" and \"Wild Draw Four\" cards\r\n\r\nEach player is dealt 7 cards and the remaining cards are placed face down to form a draw pile. The first player has to match the card in the discard pile either by number or color or the player can throw down a Wild Card else he must pick a card from the draw pile. If he can play what is drawn, great. Program support is provided on musescore.org.\r\n\r\n\r\nFeatures supported by MuseScore include:\r\n\r\n* Unlimited score length\r\n* Unlimited number of staves per system\r\n* Up to four independent voices per staff\r\n* Score creation wizard and templates\r\n* Guitar, bass, ukulele, lute tablature\r\n* Automatic part extraction and transposition\r\n* Repeats, including segnos, codas, and measure repeats\r\n* Dynamics, articulations, and other expression markings, with playback support for most\r\n* Custom text markings\r\n* Lyrics\r\n* Chord symbols\r\n* Jazz notation, including lead sheets, slash notation and a “handwritten” font for text\r\n* Swing and shuffle playback\r\n* Mixer for instrument levels and effects\r\n* Percussion notation\r\n* Early music notation\r\n* Cross-staff beaming\r\n* Import of graphics\r\n* Custom key signatures\r\n* Additive time signatures\r\n* User-defined score styles\r\n\r\nMost elements in MuseScore are laid out automatically but can also be positioned manually. The capabilities of MuseScore can be extended via plugins, and the growing repository on musescore.org contains many plugins submitted by users.\r\n\r\nMuseScore includes a set of sounds that reproduce common instruments (as defined by General MIDI) without taking up a lot of disk space or memory, but you can also substitute any SoundFont you prefer for a wider variety of sounds or for more realism.\r\n\r\nMuseScore can import and export MIDI and MusicXML files, and it can also import from Capella and several other programs.
